791|b096af|            // NOTE: We intentionally do NOT manipulate undoManager.disableUndoRegistration/enableUndoRegistration
792|bf1d61|            // here. UITextView's internal undo manager state machine is fragile and can crash with
793|b755b7|            // "enableUndoRegistration may only be invoked with matching call to disableUndoRegistration"
794|dd5c2c|            // when attributedText assignment triggers internal undo callbacks.
795|75d880|            // 
796|ff6bb4|            // Instead, we let the system handle undo naturally. The trade-off is that syntax highlighting
797|92400f|            // changes might add noise to the undo stack, but this is preferable to crashing.
798|3070d1|

800|335b1a|            textView.selectedRange = selectedRange

874|8a6136|            guard let selectedRange = textView.selectedTextRange else { return }

876|3070d1|

939|1f70dc|                parent.editorCore.editorFontSize = min(max(finalSize, 8), 32)

946|79a3a7|        // MARK: - FEAT-044 Matching Bracket Highlight
947|adc83b|
948|0ebefc|        private func updateMatchingBracketHighlight(_ textView: UITextView) {
949|95106c|            // Clear any existing highlights
950|942bd7|            if !bracketHighlightRanges.isEmpty {
951|de3115|                for r in bracketHighlightRanges {
952|fc4278|                    textView.textStorage.removeAttribute(.backgroundColor, range: r)
953|f49974|                    textView.textStorage.removeAttribute(.underlineStyle, range: r)
954|4e2d32|                }
955|9251f4|                bracketHighlightRanges.removeAll()
956|a7dc16|            }
957|adc83b|
958|fa98f8|            // Only highlight when there's a caret (no selection)
959|a5bb65|            let selection = textView.selectedRange
960|1f8f0d|            guard selection.length == 0 else { return }
961|adc83b|
962|00ec30|            let nsText = (textView.text ?? "") as NSString
963|5fd871|            let length = nsText.length
964|02d5bd|            guard length > 0 else { return }
965|adc83b|
966|03c869|            let caret = selection.location
967|adc83b|
968|3fc991|            // Candidate bracket location: char before caret, else at caret
969|3bd137|            let candidateIndices: [Int] = [
970|56ffd0|                caret - 1,
971|fba5cd|                caret
972|6421ea|            ].filter { $0 >= 0 && $0 < length }
973|adc83b|
974|fe440d|            func isBracket(_ c: unichar) -> Bool {
975|a7993e|                c == 123 || c == 125 || c == 40 || c == 41 || c == 91 || c == 93 // { } ( ) [ ]
976|a7dc16|            }
977|adc83b|
978|3ed164|            var bracketIndex: Int?
979|c2ec75|            var bracketChar: unichar = 0
980|adc83b|
981|538fcd|            for idx in candidateIndices {
982|00c134|                let c = nsText.character(at: idx)
983|149087|                if isBracket(c) {
984|ea2f0d|                    bracketIndex = idx
985|b16a8e|                    bracketChar = c
986|8dcb2c|                    break
987|4e2d32|                }
988|a7dc16|            }
989|adc83b|
990|bad712|            guard let idx = bracketIndex else { return }
991|adc83b|
992|6ef39d|            // Define bracket pairs
993|ffef8e|            let openToClose: [unichar: unichar] = [123: 125, 40: 41, 91: 93] // { -> }, ( -> ), [ -> ]
994|844dfd|            let closeToOpen: [unichar: unichar] = [125: 123, 41: 40, 93: 91] // } -> {, ) -> (, ] -> [
995|adc83b|
996|6035ba|            let theme = ThemeManager.shared.currentTheme
997|dd2745|            let bg = UIColor(theme.selection).withAlphaComponent(theme.isDark ? 0.35 : 0.22)
998|adc83b|
999|815cc6|            var matchIndex: Int?
1000|adc83b|

2228|5f3077|        }
2229|27e597|    }
2230|b4687f|    
2231|19adff|    private func highlightPattern(_ attributed: NSMutableAttributedString, pattern: String, color: UIColor, text: String, options: NSRegularExpression.Options = [], captureGroup: Int = 0) {
2232|a52e64|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: options) else { return }
2233|aa10a9|        let range = NSRange(location: 0, length: text.utf16.count)
2234|d6ed84|        
2235|3902f5|        regex.enumerateMatches(in: text, options: [], range: range) { match, _, _ in
2236|e545c6|            guard let match = match else { return }
2237|47c38f|            let matchRange = captureGroup > 0 && match.numberOfRanges > captureGroup
2238|c66c91|                ? match.range(at: captureGroup)
2239|b48e36|                : match.range
2240|aa8d3a|            if matchRange.location != NSNotFound {
2241|4030f7|                attributed.addAttribute(.foregroundColor, value: color, range: matchRange)
2242|a7dc16|            }
2243|5f3077|        }
2244|27e597|    }

1076|fcdc4d|        in textContainer: NSTextContainer,
1077|1874c5|        forGlyphRange glyphRange: NSRange
1078|54d8bb|    ) -> Bool {
1079|04c681|        guard let owner = ownerTextView,
1080|059837|              let foldingManager = owner.foldingManager,
1081|e73db4|              let fileId = owner.fileId
1082|4ebc7a|        else {
1083|e2e187|            return false
1084|5f3077|        }
1085|adc83b|
1086|9de2dc|        // Convert glyphRange -> characterRange so we can compute the line index.
1087|9471e8|        let charRange = self.characterRange(forGlyphRange: glyphRange, actualGlyphRange: nil)
1088|e786e2|        let loc = max(0, charRange.location)
1089|adc83b|
1090|b1964a|        let full = (self.textStorage?.string ?? "") as NSString
1091|ca159a|        let lineIndex = FoldingLayoutManager.lineIndex(atUTF16Location: loc, in: full)
1092|adc83b|
1093|7b763c|        if foldingManager.isLineFolded(fileId: fileId, line: lineIndex) {
1094|2e29aa|            // Collapse this visual line fragment.
1095|52dd91|            lineFragmentRect.pointee.size.height = 0
1096|3edd23|            lineFragmentUsedRect.pointee.size.height = 0
1097|eaeafe|            baselineOffset.pointee = 0
1098|40cfc4|            return true
1099|5f3077|        }
1100|adc83b|
1101|dc1500|        return false
1102|27e597|    }
1103|adc83b|
1104|8aab29|    private static func lineIndex(atUTF16Location loc: Int, in text: NSString) -> Int {
1105|470ca2|        if loc <= 0 { return 0 }
1106|adc83b|
1107|cdd09d|        let capped = min(loc, text.length)
1108|d609cf|        var line = 0
1109|d0a79c|        var searchStart = 0
1110|adc83b|
1111|bbb957|        while searchStart < capped {
1112|fc657a|            let r = text.range(of: "\n", options: [], range: NSRange(location: searchStart, length: capped - searchStart))
1113|d8b23a|            if r.location == NSNotFound { break }
1114|e2b919|            line += 1
1115|dae32a|            let next = r.location + 1
1116|af699d|            if next >= capped { break }
1117|317174|            searchStart = next
1118|5f3077|        }
1119|adc83b|
1120|bf9a21|        return line
1121|27e597|    }

251|42046c|                    startLine: lastBlock.startLine,
252|a646f4|                    endLine: lines.count - 1,
253|68bd66|                    type: lastBlock.type,
254|2cb6f6|                    label: lastBlock.label
255|2188d8|                ))
256|a7dc16|            }
257|5f3077|        }
258|d6ed84|        
259|da4698|        // Sort regions by start line
260|e60f91|        regions.sort { $0.startLine < $1.startLine }
261|d6ed84|        
262|5f2f76|        self.foldRegions = regions
263|d6ed84|        
264|3b484c|        // Store regions in the per-file dictionary
265|8c6b47|        if let fileId = currentFileId {
266|823f0a|            foldRegionsByFile[fileId] = regions
267|5f3077|        }

270|f7b7e9|        if let filePath = filePath {

272|5f3077|        }
273|d6ed84|        
274|08ca44|        updateCollapsedLines()
275|27e597|    }

279|d80e09|    private func detectRegionStart(_ line: String) -> String? {
280|2a6674|        // C# / VS style regions
281|1989c4|        if line.hasPrefix("#region") {

286|667815|        if line.hasPrefix("#pragma mark") {
287|4621b4|            let components = line.components(separatedBy: "#pragma mark")
288|fec7ec|            return components.count > 1 ? components[1].trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) : "Mark"
289|5f3077|        }
290|ccd53a|        // Swift MARK comments
291|b5e23f|        if line.contains("MARK:") {
292|504937|            let components = line.components(separatedBy: "MARK:")
293|fec7ec|            return components.count > 1 ? components[1].trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) : "Mark"
294|5f3077|        }

296|453092|        if line.contains("TODO:") {
297|a4bc68|            let components = line.components(separatedBy: "TODO:")
298|5b14a7|            return "TODO: " + (components.count > 1 ? components[1].trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) : "")
299|5f3077|        }
300|92ac0a|        if line.contains("FIXME:") {
301|0b0cff|            let components = line.components(separatedBy: "FIXME:")
302|218d1e|            return "FIXME: " + (components.count > 1 ? components[1].trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces) : "")
303|5f3077|        }

347|763883|    private func detectDeclaration(_ line: String) -> (type: FoldRegion.FoldType, label: String)? {
348|3ccee6|        func matchName(pattern: String) -> String? {
349|6cc0c4|            guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern, options: []) else { return nil }
350|f2f390|            guard let match = regex.firstMatch(in: line, range: NSRange(line.startIndex..., in: line)),
351|ebf922|                  match.numberOfRanges >= 2,
352|762e94|                  let r = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: line)
353|f5f042|            else { return nil }
354|480e4a|            return String(line[r])
355|5f3077|        }
356|adc83b|
357|f67078|        // Allow leading attributes like "@MainActor", "@available(...)"
358|0c5ed8|        // Allow common modifiers in any order (best-effort).
359|ca2c54|        let prefix = #"^(?:\s*@\w+(?:\([^\)]*\))?\s+)*(?:\s*(?:public|private|internal|fileprivate|open|final|indirect|lazy|static|override|mutating|nonmutating)\s+)*"#
360|adc83b|
361|cf49c1|        // IMPORTANT: avoid treating "class func"/"class var" as a type declaration.
362|e1fc33|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"class\s+(?!func\b|var\b|let\b)([A-Za-z_]\w*)"#) {
363|d80de1|            return (.classOrStruct, name)
364|5f3077|        }
365|adc83b|
366|8d6e9b|        // Actor (Swift concurrency) – fold like a class/struct
367|8d98f9|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"actor\s+([A-Za-z_]\w*)"#) {
368|d80de1|            return (.classOrStruct, name)
369|5f3077|        }
370|adc83b|
371|c629a9|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"struct\s+([A-Za-z_]\w*)"#) {
372|d80de1|            return (.classOrStruct, name)
373|5f3077|        }
374|adc83b|
375|75283c|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"enum\s+([A-Za-z_]\w*)"#) {
376|0f57db|            return (.enumDeclaration, name)
377|5f3077|        }
378|adc83b|
379|bb35e5|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"protocol\s+([A-Za-z_]\w*)"#) {
380|982dbc|            return (.protocolDeclaration, name)
381|5f3077|        }
382|adc83b|
383|940527|        // Extensions can include dotted names (Foo.Bar)
384|b2a8c3|        if let name = matchName(pattern: prefix + #"extension\s+([A-Za-z_][A-Za-z0-9_\.]*)"#) {
385|fbf8d2|            return (.extension, name)
386|5f3077|        }
387|adc83b|
388|c2ae65|        return nil
389|27e597|    }
390|b4687f|    
391|a1a6f6|    private func detectFunction(_ line: String) -> String? {
392|d7dbc1|        // Function detection with visibility modifiers
393|2861c1|        let visibilityKeywords = ["public", "private", "internal", "fileprivate", "static", "class", "override", "final", "mutating", "convenience"]
394|d6ed84|        
395|981adf|        // Check for 'func' keyword
396|db4a2c|        if line.contains("func ") {
397|25ca5f|            // Extract function name
398|270a0d|            let funcPattern = "func\\s+(\\w+)"
399|b5e31c|            if let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: funcPattern),
400|d7fb50|               let match = regex.firstMatch(in: line, range: NSRange(line.startIndex..., in: line)),
401|9e61c1|               let nameRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: line) {
402|456ee3|                let functionName = String(line[nameRange])
403|185b9c|                // Check for parameters to create label
404|bbf605|                if let parenStart = line.firstIndex(of: "("), let parenEnd = line.firstIndex(of: ")") {
405|2d3254|                    let params = String(line[parenStart...parenEnd])
406|929aa2|                    return "\(functionName)\(params)"
407|4e2d32|                }
408|8aa06e|                return functionName
409|a7dc16|            }
410|5f3077|        }
411|d6ed84|        
412|4d99b7|        // Init detection
413|a1d502|        if let initName = extractName(from: line, prefix: "init", visibility: visibilityKeywords) {
414|3d8f8b|            return "\(initName)"
415|5f3077|        }
416|d6ed84|        
417|2a2371|        // Deinit detection
418|70e552|        if line.contains("deinit") {
419|9db7b1|            return "deinit"
420|5f3077|        }
421|d6ed84|        
422|307e69|        // Computed property with get/set
423|f3cc39|        if line.hasPrefix("var ") && (line.contains("{") || line.contains("get")) {
424|950394|            if let varName = extractVariableName(from: line) {
425|99146d|                return varName
426|a7dc16|            }
427|5f3077|        }
428|d6ed84|        
429|c2ae65|        return nil
430|27e597|    }
431|b4687f|    
432|1ec945|    private func detectControlFlow(_ line: String) -> String? {
433|bad9a4|        let controlFlowPatterns = [
434|0bf98c|            ("if ", "if"),
435|9fe51e|            ("guard ", "guard"),
436|62af45|            ("else if", "else if"),
437|7da324|            ("else", "else"),
438|99fc8d|            ("for ", "for"),
439|37f5a4|            ("while ", "while"),
440|402c75|            ("repeat", "repeat"),
441|f81318|            ("switch ", "switch"),
442|ff609c|            ("case ", "case"),
443|d493af|            ("default:", "default"),
444|0ca7b9|            ("do ", "do"),
445|30a630|            ("catch", "catch")
446|220505|        ]
447|d6ed84|        
448|186e39|        for (pattern, label) in controlFlowPatterns {
449|3cfde0|            if line.contains(pattern) {
450|6ef273|                return label
451|a7dc16|            }
452|5f3077|        }
453|c2ae65|        return nil
454|27e597|    }
455|b4687f|    
456|143320|    private func extractName(from line: String, prefix: String, visibility: [String]) -> String? {
457|47867c|        var components = line.components(separatedBy: .whitespaces).filter { !$0.isEmpty }
458|d6ed84|        
459|b4fd50|        // Remove visibility modifiers
460|6bbc02|        components = components.filter { !visibility.contains($0) }
461|d6ed84|        
462|ad7b7d|        // Find prefix index
463|524a3a|        if let prefixIndex = components.firstIndex(where: { $0 == prefix }),
464|22dab3|           prefixIndex + 1 < components.count {
465|5c4751|            var name = components[prefixIndex + 1]
466|43f61d|            // Remove colons and other trailing characters
467|dcb9cb|            name = name.components(separatedBy: ":").first ?? name
468|3f8c05|            name = name.components(separatedBy: "<").first ?? name
469|dcb9cb|            name = name.components(separatedBy: ":").first ?? name
470|470adb|            return name
471|5f3077|        }
472|c2ae65|        return nil
473|27e597|    }
474|b4687f|    
475|c68b6f|    private func extractVariableName(from line: String) -> String? {
476|6e7aec|        let components = line.components(separatedBy: .whitespaces).filter { !$0.isEmpty }
477|a2b557|        if components.count >= 2, components[0] == "var" {
478|696097|            var varName = components[1]
479|cdb291|            varName = varName.components(separatedBy: ":").first ?? varName
480|0300ee|            varName = varName.components(separatedBy: "=").first ?? varName
481|c7c291|            return varName
482|5f3077|        }
483|c2ae65|        return nil
484|27e597|    }

512|786ea9|    /// Saves the current fold state to UserDefaults
513|1043ae|    func saveFoldState(for filePath: String) {
514|d1c5a5|        let key = UserDefaultsKeys.foldStatePrefix + filePath
515|d6ed84|        
516|1c2856|        // Use regions from the dictionary if available
517|19f890|        let regionsToSave: [FoldRegion]
518|021ffe|        if let fileId = currentFileId, let storedRegions = foldRegionsByFile[fileId] {
519|b1db84|            regionsToSave = storedRegions
520|b31999|        } else {
521|210675|            regionsToSave = foldRegions
522|5f3077|        }
523|d6ed84|        
524|c424a6|        // Create a simplified representation for storage
525|40fb34|        let foldState = regionsToSave.map { FoldStateEntry(startLine: $0.startLine, isFolded: $0.isFolded) }
526|d6ed84|        
527|284b9a|        if let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(foldState) {
528|d8ca2f|            UserDefaults.standard.set(data, forKey: key)
529|5f3077|        }
530|27e597|    }
531|b4687f|    
532|171d6b|    /// Restores fold state from UserDefaults
533|710040|    private func restoreFoldState(for filePath: String) {
534|d1c5a5|        let key = UserDefaultsKeys.foldStatePrefix + filePath
535|d6ed84|        
536|d7f816|        guard let data = UserDefaults.standard.data(forKey: key),
537|9cfa7e|              let foldState = try? JSONDecoder().decode([FoldStateEntry].self, from: data) else {
538|bef5d6|            return
539|5f3077|        }
540|d6ed84|        
541|f0448e|        // Apply saved state to current regions
542|9663b0|        for savedState in foldState {
543|65fcdc|            if let index = foldRegions.firstIndex(where: { $0.startLine == savedState.startLine }) {
544|7dfd32|                foldRegions[index].isFolded = savedState.isFolded
545|a7dc16|            }
546|5f3077|        }
547|27e597|    }

626|0a42c8|        }).min(by: { ($0.endLine - $0.startLine) < ($1.endLine - $1.startLine) }) {
627|acad0e|            collapseRegion(at: region.startLine)
628|5f3077|        }

636|294d4c|        }) {

638|5f3077|        }

Now I've found the root cause. The problem is:

1. **`detectFoldableRegions` is NEVER called** - The fold regions are never populated, so `isFoldable()` always returns false and no fold chevrons appear
2. **Layout is not invalidated after fold state changes** - Even if regions were populated, the `FoldingLayoutManager` needs its layout invalidated to re-render collapsed lines

Let me fix this by:
1. Calling `detectFoldableRegions` when text is loaded
2. Invalidating layout after fold operations



---

Now I understand the issues. Let me trace through the complete problem:

**Problems identified:**

1. **`detectFoldableRegions` is never called** - The fold regions dictionary is empty, so `isFoldable` always returns false
2. **Fold commands don't know the cursor line** - `handleFold` calls `foldCurrentLine()` which doesn't get the actual cursor position
3. **Layout not invalidated after fold changes** - Even if regions were populated, the `FoldingLayoutManager` isn't told to re-layout after fold state changes

Let me fix these issues:



---

Now I understand the issues. Let me trace through what I've found:

**Issue 1: `detectFoldableRegions()` is NEVER CALLED**
The CodeFoldingManager has `foldRegions` and `foldRegionsByFile` but they're always empty because `detectFoldableRegions(in:filePath:)` is never invoked. The gutter checks `isFoldable()` which always returns false.

**Issue 2: Layout Not Invalidated After Fold**
Even if fold state changes, the `FoldingLayoutManager` isn't told to re-layout. TextKit caches layout and won't re-run the delegate method.

Let me fix both issues:



---

Now I understand the issue. Let me trace through the problems:

**Problem 1:** `detectFoldableRegions` is NEVER called, so `foldRegions` is always empty - no fold regions exist to fold/unfold.

**Problem 2:** Even when fold state changes, the `FoldingLayoutManager` isn't told to re-layout - so even if regions existed, visual folding wouldn't happen.

**Problem 3:** The `foldCurrentLine()` and `unfoldCurrentLine()` methods fold the first region, not the one at the cursor.

Let me fix all three issues:

Now I understand. The FoldingLayoutManager exists and works correctly - it checks `isLineFolded` and collapses lines. But the issue is:

1. **Layout isn't invalidated when fold state changes** - TextKit caches layout
2. **Keyboard shortcuts don't pass cursor position** - `foldCurrentLine()` just folds first available region

Let me fix both issues. First, let me add a method to FoldingLayoutManager to invalidate layout:



---

3: /// TextKit layout manager that collapses line fragments for lines marked folded in CodeFoldingManager.
4: /// This is a view-level folding implementation (it does NOT modify the underlying text).
5: 
6: final class FoldingLayoutManager: NSLayoutManager, NSLayoutManagerDelegate {
7:     weak var ownerTextView: EditorTextView?
8:     private var foldingObserver: NSObjectProtocol?
9: 
10:     override init() {
11:         super.init()
12:         self.delegate = self
13:         setupFoldingObserver()
14:     }
15: 
16:     required init?(coder: NSCoder) {
17:         super.init(coder: coder)
18:         self.delegate = self
19:         setupFoldingObserver()
20:     }
21: 
22:     deinit {
23:         if let observer = foldingObserver {
24:             NotificationCenter.default.removeObserver(observer)
25:         }
26:     }
27: 
28:     private func setupFoldingObserver() {
29:         foldingObserver = NotificationCenter.default.addObserver(
30:             forName: .codeFoldingDidChange,
31:             object: nil,
32:             queue: .main
33:         ) { [weak self] _ in
34:             self?.invalidateFoldingLayout()
35:         }
36:     }
37: 
38: 
39:     func layoutManager(
40:         _ layoutManager: NSLayoutManager,
41:         shouldSetLineFragmentRect lineFragmentRect: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGRect>,
42:         lineFragmentUsedRect: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGRect>,
43:         baselineOffset: UnsafeMutablePointer<CGFloat>,
44:         in textContainer: NSTextContainer,
45:         forGlyphRange glyphRange: NSRange
46:     ) -> Bool {
47:         guard let owner = ownerTextView,
48:               let foldingManager = owner.foldingManager,
49:               let fileId = owner.fileId
50:         else {
51:             return false
52:         }
53: 
54:         // Convert glyphRange -> characterRange so we can compute the line index.
55:         let charRange = self.characterRange(forGlyphRange: glyphRange, actualGlyphRange: nil)
56:         let loc = max(0, charRange.location)
57: 
58:         let full = (self.textStorage?.string ?? "") as NSString
59:         let lineIndex = FoldingLayoutManager.lineIndex(atUTF16Location: loc, in: full)
60: 
61:         if foldingManager.isLineFolded(fileId: fileId, line: lineIndex) {
62:             // Collapse this visual line fragment.
63:             lineFragmentRect.pointee.size.height = 0
64:             lineFragmentUsedRect.pointee.size.height = 0
65:             baselineOffset.pointee = 0
66:             return true
67:         }
68: 
69:         return false
70:     }
71: 
72:     private static func lineIndex(atUTF16Location loc: Int, in text: NSString) -> Int {
73:         if loc <= 0 { return 0 }
74: 
75:         let capped = min(loc, text.length)
76:         var line = 0
77:         var searchStart = 0
78: 
79:         while searchStart < capped {
80:             let r = text.range(of: "\n", options: [], range: NSRange(location: searchStart, length: capped - searchStart))
81:             if r.location == NSNotFound { break }
82:             line += 1
83:             let next = r.location + 1
84:             if next >= capped { break }
85:             searchStart = next
86:         }
87: 
88:         return line
89:     }
90: 
91:     /// Invalidate layout to reflect fold state changes.
92:     /// Call this after toggling fold regions.
93:     func invalidateFoldingLayout() {
94:         guard let textStorage = self.textStorage else { return }
95:         let fullRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: textStorage.length)
96:         self.invalidateLayout(forCharacterRange: fullRange, actualCharacterRange: nil)
97:         self.invalidateDisplay(forCharacterRange: fullRange)
98:     }
99: }

>>>REPORT
## Code Folding UI Fix - Complete

### Root Causes Identified

1. **`detectFoldableRegions` was never called** - The fold regions dictionary was always empty, so `isFoldable()` always returned false and no fold chevrons appeared in the gutter.

2. **Keyboard shortcuts used wrong fold methods** - `handleFold`/`handleUnfold` called `foldCurrentLine()`/`unfoldCurrentLine()` which don't use the actual cursor position.

3. **Layout not invalidated after fold state changes** - The `FoldingLayoutManager` was never told to re-layout after fold operations, so collapsed lines wouldn't visually hide.

### Changes Made

**1. SplitEditorView.swift (lines 671-679):**
- Added `foldingManager.detectFoldableRegions(in: text, filePath: fileId)` in `.onAppear` and `.onChange(of: tab.id)` to populate fold regions when files are opened or switched.

**2. SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift (lines 910-920):**
- Changed `handleFold` to use `CodeFoldingManager.shared.foldAtLine(cursorLine)` with actual cursor position
- Changed `handleUnfold` to use `CodeFoldingManager.shared.unfoldAtLine(cursorLine)` with actual cursor position

**3. CodeFoldingManager.swift (lines 67-70, 858-859):**
- Added `Notification.Name.codeFoldingDidChange` extension
- Modified `updateCollapsedLines()` to post notification after updating collapsed lines

**4. FoldingLayoutManager.swift (lines 8, 13, 19, 22-36):**
- Added `foldingObserver` property to track notification observer
- Added `setupFoldingObserver()` called from both `init()` methods
- Added `deinit` to clean up observer
- Observer listens for `.codeFoldingDidChange` and calls `invalidateFoldingLayout()`

### How It Works Now

1. When a file is opened → `detectFoldableRegions` is called → fold regions are populated → gutter shows fold chevrons
2. User clicks chevron or uses Cmd+Opt+[ → `toggleFold`/`foldAtLine` is called → fold state changes → `updateCollapsedLines()` posts notification
3. `FoldingLayoutManager` receives notification → `invalidateFoldingLayout()` is called → TextKit re-renders with collapsed line heights = 0
4. Gutter also updates because `foldingManager` is `@ObservableObject` and SwiftUI re-renders

### Files Modified
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/SplitEditorView.swift`
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/SyntaxHighlightingTextView.swift`
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Services/CodeFoldingManager.swift`
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/FoldingLayoutManager.swift`
